  629|    398|        }
  630|       |
  631|    398|        if !started {
  632|     44|            if ch == '/' {
  633|     33|                started = true;
  634|     33|                sample.push(ch);
  635|     33|            }
                          ^11
  636|     44|            continue;
  637|    354|        }
  638|       |
  639|    324|        match ch {
  640|     10|            '[' => {
  641|     10|                consume_regex_char_class(&mut chars);
  642|     10|                sample.push('x');
  643|     10|                consume_regex_quantifier(&mut chars);
  644|     10|            }
  645|       |            '.' => {
  646|      4|                if sample_is_absolute_url_host(&sample) {
  647|      2|                    sample.push('.');
  648|      2|                } else {
  649|      2|                    sample.push('x');
  650|      2|                }
  651|      4|                consume_regex_quantifier(&mut chars);
  652|       |            }
  653|     15|            '$' => break,
  654|       |            '|' | '(' | ')' => {
  655|      1|                unsupported = true;
  656|      1|                break;
  657|       |            }

                          ^323                         ^323 ^323   ^323 ^323
  659|       |            _ => {
  660|      1|                unsupported = true;
  661|      1|                break;
  662|       |            }
  663|       |        }
  664|       |    }
  665|       |
  666|     39|    if !unsupported && is_candidate_url(&sample) {
                                     ^34              ^34
  667|     31|        Some(sample)
  668|       |    } else {
  669|      8|        None
  670|       |    }

  673|     10|fn consume_regex_char_class(chars: &mut std::iter::Peekable<std::str::Chars<'_>>) {
  674|     10|    let mut escaped = false;
  675|     78|    for next in chars.by_ref() {
                              ^10   ^10
  676|     78|        if escaped {
  677|      1|            escaped = false;
  678|      1|            continue;
  679|     77|        }
  680|     77|        if next == '\\' {
  681|      1|            escaped = true;
  682|      1|            continue;
  683|     76|        }
  684|     76|        if next == ']' {
  685|     10|            break;
  686|     66|        }
  687|       |    }

  690|     14|fn consume_regex_quantifier(chars: &mut std::iter::Peekable<std::str::Chars<'_>>) {
  691|     27|    while matches!(chars.peek(), Some('+' | '*' | '?' | '{')) {
                        ^14
  692|     13|        let quantifier = chars.next();

  694|      4|            for next in chars.by_ref() {
                                      ^1    ^1
  695|      4|                if next == '}' {
  696|      1|                    break;
  697|      3|                }
  698|       |            }
  699|     12|        }
  700|       |    }

                                                ^2       ^47

  712|      2|        return false;
  713|       |    };

 1062|      1|    fn marks_urls_inside_skipped_and_conditional_tests() {

 1069|      1|                test('conditional wrapper', async ({ page }) => {

 1271|    231|fn playwright_selector_regex(attribute: &str) -> Regex {
 1272|    231|    let pattern = format!(
 1273|       |        r#"\[\s*{}\s*(=|\^=|\$=|\*=)\s*(?:"([^"]+)"|'([^']+)')\s*\]"#,
 1274|    231|        regex::escape(attribute)

 1279|     42|fn matcher_for_operator(operator: &str, value: &str) -> SelectorMatcher {
 1280|     42|    match operator {
 1281|     42|        "^=" => SelectorMatcher::Prefix(value.to_string()),
                              ^7
 1282|     35|        "$=" => SelectorMatcher::Suffix(value.to_string()),
                              ^3
 1283|     32|        "*=" => SelectorMatcher::Contains(value.to_string()),
                              ^4
 1284|     28|        _ => SelectorMatcher::Exact(value.to_string()),
 1285|       |    }

 1294|     11|fn template_parts(source: &str) -> Vec<String> {
 1295|     11|    let mut parts = Vec::new();
 1296|     11|    let mut rest = source;
 1297|     20|    while let Some(start) = rest.find("${") {
                                 ^10
 1298|     10|        parts.push(rest[..start].to_string());

 1300|     10|        let Some(end) = expression.find('}') else {
                               ^9
 1301|      1|            return vec![source.to_string()];
 1302|       |        };
 1303|      9|        rest = &expression[end + 1..];
 1304|       |    }
 1305|     10|    parts.push(rest.to_string());
 1306|     10|    parts

 2020|      1|    fn identifier_reassignment_uses_identifier_boundaries_and_assignment_operator() {
 2021|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw = makeId();", "dataPw"));
 2022|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment(
 2023|      1|            "data$Pw = makeId();",
 2024|      1|            "data$Pw"
 2025|       |        ));
 2026|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment("xdataPw = 1;", "dataPw"));
 2027|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment("dataPwx = 1;", "dataPw"));
 2028|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw = 1;", "dataPw"));
 2029|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw += 1;", "dataPw"));
 2030|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw++", "dataPw"));
 2031|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("++dataPw", "dataPw"));
 2032|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw += '-x';", "dataPw"));
 2033|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment(
 2034|      1|            "dataPw ??= makeId();",
 2035|      1|            "dataPw"
 2036|       |        ));
 2037|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw++;", "dataPw"));
 2038|      1|        assert!(has_identifier_reassignment("--dataPw;", "dataPw"));
 2039|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw === 'save';", "dataPw"));
 2040|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment("dataPw == 'save';", "dataPw"));
 2041|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment(
 2042|      1|            "// dataPw = makeId();\nconst message = \"dataPw += '-x';\";",
 2043|      1|            "dataPw"
 2044|      1|        ));
 2045|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment("userid = makeId();", "id"));
 2046|      1|        assert!(!has_identifier_reassignment("id => id", "id"));
 2047|      1|    }
